[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify Root Cause[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer binaries [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are built by Meson [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut are never â€œinstalledâ€ via Mesonâ€™s install mechanism, because their [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` declarations lack `install: true`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Downstream OSS-Fuzz packaging relies on `meson install` to populate `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWithout `install: true`, Meson skips these targets, so the OSS-Fuzz scripts fall [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback to ad-hoc copying [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`cp`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which, under default umasks or mount semantics, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrips the execute bit, leading to Bash exit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Affected targets:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m69[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Required Changes[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block, add the parameters:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       â€¢ `install: true`  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       â€¢ `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       â€¢ Optionally `install_mode: [0m[32m'0755'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough Meson defaults to a sensible [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable mode when installing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This will cause `meson install` to copy the binaries into the standard bindir [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with executable permissions preserved.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `dav1d_fuzzer` target and modify its `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocation to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minclude:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      install     : true,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      install_dir : [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      install_mode: [0m[32m'0755'[0m[39m,[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Repeat for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Verify that no other fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `build_by_default`, `dependencies`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltered.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz build script [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`meson setup â€¦ && meson install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` is now present with executable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`rwx`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bits.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preservation of Critical Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing compiler flags [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`c_args`, `link_args`, `link_with`, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dependencies`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and build semantics remain untouched.  [0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that the fuzzer binary in the container at `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` has [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to runtime logic or harness; negligible performance or behavior [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimpact.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer binaries `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` are built by Meson [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut never installed into the `$OUT` directory, so the Docker runnerâ€™s `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` mount [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlacks an executable copy. As a result, invoking `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` yields [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit status [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m because the file either does not exist there [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor lacks the execute bit.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In contrast, the main CLI `dav1d` target is marked with `install: true`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring it lands in `$PREFIX/bin` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand thus in `$OUT` once Ninja install runs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzers need analogous `install` directives.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Overview[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` to instruct Meson to install both fuzzers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the root of the install prefix. This will cause `ninja install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOSS-Fuzz build harness runs after `ninja`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to copy the executables, with correct [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermissions, into `$OUT`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifically, for each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` declaration of the fuzzers:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ Add `install: true`  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ Add `install_dir: [0m[32m''[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mempty string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to place the binaries directly under [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT` rather than under a subdirectory like `bin/`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change preserves all existing compilation and linking flags, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies, and multi-threaded fuzzing logic. It only affects post-build [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallation steps, ensuring the runner sees valid, executable binaries.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the stanza for `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Update it to:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[32m''[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Locate the stanza for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m69[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Update it similarly:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[32m''[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Save changes and re-run the OSS-Fuzz build [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ninja && ninja install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Ensure[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat both `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` appear with execute [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermissions.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By mirroring the `install: true` pattern used for the main `dav1d` binary, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer executables will be installed into the `$OUT` directory. This addresses the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission deniedâ€ immediately at container startup, since `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now exist and be executable.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach does not modify any harness or fuzzing logic, preserving [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and the fuzzerâ€™s multi-threaded behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external dependencies or utilities are altered; the only modification is in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Meson build definition.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the empty `install_dir` were misinterpreted by an older Meson, binaries [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcould end up in an unexpected directory. However, current OSS-Fuzz images bundle a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson version fully supporting `install_dir: [0m[32m''[0m[39m`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change is made to source-level logic, so runtime behavior under libFuzzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains unchanged.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After applying, verify in a local Docker repro that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` has[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits execute bit [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-rwxr-xr-x`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before attempting fuzz runs.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This single change ensures the fuzzer binaries are present and executable in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Docker runnerâ€™s `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` mount, resolving exit status [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m with minimal [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvasiveness and full compatibility with the existing fuzzing harness and test [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuite.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Docker fuzzer runner mounts the OSS-Fuzz `$OUT` directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpopulated by [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Meson build/install[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` inside the container. It then invokes [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`. The fuzzer binary is present but lacks the execute bit, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing â€œPermission denied.â€  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the Meson files under `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, the two fuzzers [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are declared with `build_by_default: true` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut **no** `install: true`. Consequently, the OSS-Fuzz build scripts do not install[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem into `$OUT` via `ninja install`, and the fallback copy logic in the Python [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrapper ends up producing a non-executable file.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edit `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For both `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madd:  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       â€¢ `install: true` to mark the target for installation  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       â€¢ `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` so that the resulting executables land directly in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallation prefix root [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`$OUT/`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matching the runnerâ€™s expectation of [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[39m<fuzzer_name>`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m, â€¦[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block:  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after `build_by_default: true,` insert:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `install: true,`  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m,`  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, â€¦[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block:  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after `build_by_default: true,` insert:  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `install: true,`  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m,`  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Save and re-run the OSS-Fuzz build. The build scripts will now invoke `ninja [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall`, placing `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` into `$OUT/` with correct [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0755[0m[39m permissions.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding `install: true` integrates these fuzzers into Mesonâ€™s install step, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich OSS-Fuzz will call automatically [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor detect[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of its fallback copy [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Setting `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` places the binaries in `$OUT/` root, satisfying [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`run_fuzzer`â€™s hard-coded invocation of `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change is local to the Meson build files; it does not alter any fuzzing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic, harness scripts, or external dependencies. It preserves all existing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and tests.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing native [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-fuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m installation paths are affected, because the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew install directives apply only under `tests/libfuzzer`.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is to the fuzzer artifacts, ensuring they become executable. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDownstream packaging or PATH assumptions remain untouched.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `tools/meson.build`, the main CLI target uses `install: true` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m122[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWe mirror that pattern here for the fuzzers.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This aligns with Mesonâ€™s standard install semantics and OSS-Fuzzâ€™s meson-based[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild recipes.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:    link_with : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlibdav1d, dav1d_input_objs, dav1d_output_objs[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:    include_directories : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdav1d_inc_dirs[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:        getopt_dependency,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:        thread_dependency,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:        rt_dependency,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:        libm_dependency,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m121[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m122[0m[39m:    install : true,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m123[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer executables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are built by [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson but never marked for installation. In OSS-Fuzzâ€™s Meson-based build flow, only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets with `install: true` are copied into the `$OUT` directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequently mounted into the runner[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the proper executable permission bits. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWithout `install: true`, Meson leaves these binaries out of `$OUT` or installs them[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith default [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-executable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m file modes, leading to the â€œPermission deniedâ€ error [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` is invoked.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Affects two executable definitions:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ Lines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ Lines [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m69[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno harness code changes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` stanza and insert `install: [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue` among its keyword arguments.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` stanza and similarly add [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true`.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure the patch targets only those two calls; leave all other arguments [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `build_by_default`, `c_args`, `link_args`, `kwargs`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intact.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Run:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```bash[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      meson setup builddir --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=[0m[32m"$DESTDIR"[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ninja -C builddir install[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to confirm that both `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` now [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappear in the output directory with the `-rwxr-xr-x` permission bits.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns with existing patterns: the CLI tool `dav1d` in `tools/meson.build` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready uses `install: true`.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Guarantees the fuzzer binaries are deployed into `$OUT` and remain executable,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout altering fuzz harness logic or test code.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves threading, compilation flags, and linkage setup exactly as [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeforeâ€”only the installation step is enabled.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validation & Side-Effects[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After rebuilding, invoking `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` should no longer yield [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission denied.â€  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzzing logic, test corpus handling, or external dependencies.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No risk of hiding other errors since we do not modify exception handling or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness scripts.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retains existing functionality and enables seamless integration with [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOSS-Fuzzâ€™s `run_fuzzer` wrapper.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reference pattern:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```meson[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d'[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[39m, install: true[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m([0m[39mseen in `tools/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:109[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m123[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apply the same `install: true` keyword for tester executables.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith this patch, the fuzzer targets will be correctly installed into `$OUT` with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable permissions, resolving the exit-[0m[1;36m126[0m[39m â€œPermission deniedâ€ error without [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimpacting any other part of the codebase.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
